chaunge brother vnto brother lyke ſtraungers noon knewe thentent myne auctour trowith aduerſite ther gilt cauſyd vengeaunce elles god right equyte diſpoſith hath ordenaunce amonge theym ſo greate goddes worſhip paynymes wyſe founder rightes falſe ſacrifice towarde perce chees dwellynge place cuntre orient lordſhip ſhulde ſtretche greate ſpace boundyd occident perce lande hath extent towarde party rede ſee londe perce ſo liſt ſe bochas olde remembre put mynde howe perce coſtith enuyron septemtrion greate ynde many myghty region nembroth hadde firſt dominacion extēdith bokes ſpecifie oute ſharpe hungre worldly habundaunce makynge maner reſemblaunce tantalus whan ye deppeſt ſynke nature mooſt thruſtleugh drynke clymbeth higheſt fortune whele ſodenly richeſſis doth aſcende vnware turne afore ſeen neueradell whan leeſt weneth maketh deſcende fro ſuch chaungys may ſilf defende pouert nat diſmayde litell holde theym ſilf appayde howe kinge hoſtilius worſhippynge fals goddys conſumpte fiery leuene bochas gan muſe matere conſidred firſt worldly thinge muſt faile wepynge • yen dyd appere princis whilom famous itayle gan fall full pitouſly bewaile contrarye fallinge lowe tofore myſcheef knowe vncouth thilke aduerſite namely prince whan ſodeyn euer haue lyued proſꝑite hauynge fortune mater compleyne wretch lyueth ay payne cuſtum cauſeth conceyued ſentence ioy ſorowe full greate difference ioye paſſyd newe remembraunce whan folke fall felilicite treble wiſe doth theym greate greuaunce vnware turne tranquilite vnſure truſt mutabilite worldly power haue founde vnto hertis yeueth greuous wounde wretch wretchidneſſe hath euer lyued neuer partable welfare wylfulneſſe neuer founde fortune fauourable ſorowe myſcheef ſo cuſtomable paynes longe contynuance doth greuys maner allegaunce prince ſat ſo high aloft ſodeyne fall mooſt contrarious deſcendynge wele vnſoft tryumphes thy glorious recorde take kinge hoſtilius rome roiall ſtall whan ſat crowned mooſt ſodenly fall remembred olde nat newe rome lorde ſire firſt kinges weryd purpyl hewe cyte gouerned empire fortune liſt deſire tyll fyll regalye frowarde dedly maladye paynes finde allegaunce temple went pylgrymage offringe made deuout obeyſaunce wherby ſumdell paynes dyd aſwage reſtoryd corage felt ſilf dyd amende comon profite ageyn gan entende vpon talbanys regnynge glorye greate auaile rome cyte knighthode greate victorye full greate cruelte beraft theym fraunchiſe lyberte made theym high renoun rome vnder ſubiection conqueſt ſtory doth deuyſe nobleſſe full ſtatly roiall gan make riche ſacrifiſe queme pleaſe memoriall rightes cerymonyall iubiter full greate reuerence afore auters fire encence inwarde entent circumſtaunces oblacion recheles founde alſo neglygent ſome frowarde fals affeccion goddys caught indignacion ſodenly deſcendynge heuene conſumpte firy leuene fals goddys might nat auaile iupiter saturnus venus let criſten defye ſuch raſcaile oure feith contrarious amonge goddys thinge mooſt outraious whan prince blent folye liſt erthly thinges falſly deifie vnto god hatefull odible withdrawynge reuerence magnifye thinges corruptible vndue honoure fals concupiſcence wherfore ye prince ware high prudence leſt god vnwarly punyſſh nobleſſe make erth fals god goddeſſe howe anchus kinge rome murdrid lucynyo thaſſent wif thinke achus kinge rome toun ſo noble ſhyninge glorye weryd crowne full famous renoun next hoſtilius put memorye wan palme many greate victorye full ſharpe knyfe murdred aſſentinge wife loued hir beſt aboue eche creature conſidred nat hir flatere falſneſſe hir double menynge vnder couerture falſly blent princis worthyneſſe robbe reue greate richeſſe hir laboure counterfete pleſaunce hir entent bringe myſchaunce anchus greate affeccion vnto goddis make ſacrifiſes augment relegion paganyſme made ſundry wiſes manhode circumſpect diuiſes vpon latynes rebell cyte comon profite made greate arme one citees called polotone knightly wan maugre al might whan theym full victorye abode lengre anone forth right made al people euery mannys ſight pryſoners romayn champion brought afore bounde toun eke finde anchus nolde cece comon profite affeccion teritories augment encrece cuntrees aboute enuyron towarde ryuere tybre renneth place lete edifie full ſtronge cite called oſtye nat withſtandynge worthyneſſe depryued ſtory telleth ſoo kingdom greate richeſſe foreyne called lucynyo wife tarquild aſſented therto whoos outrage gredy couetiſe anchus murdred full cruell wiſe howe lucynyo murdred anchus murdred thus fro whele fortune fall lucynyo rome crowned kinge romayns dyd call tarquyn olde recorde writynge hath ateyned fraudolent werkynge ſubtyll forgyd eloquence vnto theſtate roiall excellence firſt ordeyned eſtate roiall turneis iuſtes caſtellys citees playes called marciall many famous greate ſolempnytees seſſions ſtatys degree tarquyn eke firſt dyd peyne opyn ſtretys tauernes ordeyne eke preſerue cite oute doubte ennemyes lyſt theym aſſayle firſt walled rome aboute myghty toures vnlykly fayle alſo many ſtronge batayle sabynes rebellyon made theym ſubget vnto rome toun aſſented depryue worthy anchus eſtate roiall toke tanquyld vnto wyue ſlough hir lorde treaſon ful mortall god wolde right ſhuld haue fall lorde wyll nat euery thinge may ſee suffre murdre longe ſecre lucynyo greate offence touchinge murdre kynge anchus iſlayne ſodeyn vyolence two ſhipperdys ſtory telleth thus entent contrarious atwene ſilf fayned ſtrif finde weye reue life kinge ſate iugement vpon quarel iuſtiſe full ſodenly beynge aſſent fyll vpon full cruell wiſe axe ſtory doth deuiſe one theym man toke hede two ꝑtyes roof kinges hede thinge done procurynge two childre ſonnes anchus exiled falſe compaſſinge lucynyo ageyne theym mooſt yrous preſence ſo odious ſhope though oute ſight faders deth auenge myyht nature blode wyll auengyd recompence wronge kinrede chaptre like ye may ſe blode ſhed blode thus dyd blede example lete prince take hede howe murdre done ſupplantacion requyreth vengeaunce fynall guyrdon lenuoye tragedie clere inſpeccion openly declareth ſubſtaunce howe ſlaughter prince cauſeth ſubucion realmys cytees put oute ordenaunce mortall werre longe contynuaunce blode ſupplantynge ſhed kinges tweyne exaumple ſhewed fals murdre reſtreyne fyne declarynge murdre fals treſon dede horrible cryeth ay vengeaunce god aboue caſt • yen doun punyſſh ſynne mighty puiſſaūce modre myſcheef myſchaunce wherfore ye princys ſum lawe ordeyne within youre boūdis thre vice reſtreyne vice ſclaundre murdre poyſon euer theſe thre haue aqueyntaunce bringe ſorowe deſolacion put preef newe remembraunce falſhede vſed vndre faire countenaunce wherfore ye prince youre beſy peyne within youre boundys theſe vice reſtreyne god defende noble region theſe thre vice haue allyaunce ſleaundre firſte deuoureth high renoun ſleeth gode fame throug fals dalliaunce harme done late foloweth repentaunce wherfore ye prince doo lawe ordeyne punyſſh malice fals tunges reſtreyne god hath murdre abhominacion fals poyſon doth diſpleſaunce peyne compariſon condigne murdre peyſyd balaunce wherfore ye prince make ordenaunce within youre boundes ſome preuy peyne due punyſſhinge fals murdre reſtreyne noble prince prouide reaſon ageyne theſe vice make purueaunce rigoure ſhewe due execucion laboure hertely inſtaunce let deth vnder thy lordſhip thy gouernaunce collatyn lorde true huſbonde beſt beloued hole affeccion wyll quarell take honde wiſe take none accion withoute thou liſt enclyne doun goodly thyn erys yeue audience may alſo bere caſtell doun bylde freſſhly ſight exile man oute region reuoke wronge right man hath power myght reſtore paleys virgynall chaſtite whan broken wall men may alſo put oute ſeruiſe officer remeue place day whan fortune liſt diuiſe may ageyne reſtoryd grace nouther tyme ſet ſpace neuir ſtory nouther redde ſeyne maydenhede loſt recured ageyne men ſhulde haue conſcience rewe herte repente ſore haue remors greate offence rauyſſh thinge may na reſtore ſaide hath ſayde ful yore emeraude grene ꝑfight chaſtite stolne onys away may nat recured hard rauyſſhe treſoure nature nat recuꝑable lordſhyp may nat kinge emperoure refourme thinge nat refourmable ruſt diffame nat inſeꝑable maydenhede loſt newe yore man alyue may ageyne roſ • ore romayns olde pacience suffred tirauntys tyrannyes cite greate violence peple oppreſſe robbery punyſſh ſet ſtreyte eſpyes fals ••• utours well couth wydowes rauyſſhe maydens ther youth vpon mater ſtory bereth wytneſſe touchinge thexil kinge tarquinius afore rehercyd wrytinge full expreſſe hatefull deth apius • laudius treſpas done virgineus iugementys rehercyd peyne fro offyce depryued bothe tweyne nat cite whilom deſolat synachites ribaudye one ſichen gan greate debate heue accompliſſhed foule lecherye whan yonge dyna bokes ſpecifie went recheleſly walkynge vp doun ſe maydens royall toun whan sychen dyna dyd eſpye sool hir ſilf walke cyte • e began anone aſſayle hir mayſtrye aforce hir virgynyte bycauſe ſhe leyſer flee whoos greate offence tranſgreſſion cyte brought vnto diſtruccion hir fader iacob hooly hir kinrede ageyne sichen gan inwardly diſdeyne whan furye mar mooſt drede venged dyd beſy peyne ſpecially hir worthy brethern tweyne fyll cyte symeon leuy auenge ſuſter ſtroy fynally mortally gan theym ſtryue ſwerdys grounde ſharpe kene male child left none alyue ſo vengeable furious lene sychanytes might nat ſuſtene day ageyne theym ſtonde diffence importable violence god liſt punyſſh man right mortall ſwerde farwele riſiſtence whan grace faileth force goth awey myght febleth prince magnificence chaunge power impotence reuerſeth kinges ſtatly regalye exaumple sichen fals auoutrye harde dredfull punycion one princis treſpas lecherye cauſed afore god region deſtroyed withoute remedye ſtory tolde exemplifye whan noble prince wymen theym ſubmitte grace fauoure anone doth theym flye mater ſhulde write geneſis reſidue ye may rede deth sichen kinge emor howe kingdome deſtroyed dede sychanytes lo finall mede lecherye fals pleſaunce many realme hath brought vnto miſcha • ſhulde eft rherce ageyne write fals habundaunce worldly good greate caſe richeſſe folke ſet hooly pleſaunce folowe luſtys frowarde wilfulneſſe hath cauſed londes greate miſcheef diſtreſſe whan vicious life corages dyd encombre deſtroyed kingdom peple oute noumbre whan people fals obſtynacye indurate amende theym correct wyll nat tourne theym theyr lechery ay red • ſoulys enfect vnto purpos ſtyle wyll directe exaumplifye howe gabaa toun ſynnes brought confuſion whilom people called gabonytes beniamyn deſcendyd lyne ay diſpoſyd folowe theyr delites cuſtome wittes dyd enclyne worldly plente floure ſhyne dempt alwey theym mooſt due wylfulneſſe luſtys ſue lecherye ſet pleſaunce vice lad mooſt lyf wherby brought vnto myſchaunce many ſlayne full mortall ſtrife whan leuyte cam forby wife full excellent fetures beutye toke lodgynge thermophiles perciens began firſt viage knightly caſt ſtop paſſage murdre xerſes outwarde vnknowe howe artabanus treſon wrought tyll afterwarde within litell throwe newe forged oute ſought fals odious traynes neuer thought told artaxerſes gan rowne howe darye caſt occupie crowne howe deth xerſes ordeyned darye none wight wherupon ought compleyned artaxerſes prouyded anone right ſlaughtre darie ſo ageyne right yonge brother innocence falſly ſlayne dyd none offence ¶ye wite treſon compaſſed twene brother theyne make diuiſion yonger ſlayne thinge treſpaſſed mooſt redy wey deſtruccion artaxerſes concluſion whan brother murdred dede artabanus thought ſuccede artaxerſes pleyne inſtruccion one called baccarus toknes knewe couert fals treaſon forſaide double artabanus howe treynes outragious xerſes ſlayne ye haue herde forne darye appechyd wherby lorne vncouth ſtraunge treſon wrought whan artaxerſes knowlegynge greate aduys weyes hath ſought artabanus brynge vnto rekenynge ſpecially dred one thinge feble bringe thinge aboute ſeuene ſonnes ſo greate doute accompliſſh fully entent full ſecrely ordenaunce worthy hath letter ſent dwellynge perce vnder obeyſaunce withoute excuſe lenger attendaunce armyd echon eſpeciall come haſt vnto court royall cauſe comynge nat knowe kinges purpos holden ſecre kept ſo cloos high lowe menynge man pryue except kinge ſayde wolde ſee noumbre men come nede diffence might gadre lede amonge cam artabanus vnto court liſt nat fayle man cruell coragious full ſleightes gouernayle thilke tyme armed mayle none armoure ladde saue backe haburion hadde artaxarſes beynge ſtrength abrayde fals affeccion mayle wanteth length wolde chaunge myn haburion tother hauynge none euyll ſuſpeccion vngyrt ſilf wolde lenger byde ſwerde dagger caſt theym ferre aſide threwe haburion mayle ſtopped ſight beynge nakyd ſhort concluſion kinge oute pulleth ſwerde kene bright herte roue anone right indignacion toke ſeuene ſonnes caſt theym priſon ende ſhulde endite deth make degreſſion god may vengeaunce reſpite murdre wyll oute ſuch treſon artaban condicion falſly murdre ye tofore haue ſeyne vnware murdre gwerdoned ageyne thus euer murdre requireth wage sclaundre importable odious worde diffamous mooſt foule langages ſounde horrible report appere clyps duringe whoos derkeneſſe may nat clere worde murdre mooſt ougly vnfaire reherſinge infecteth aire duke palantes spartenois werred th • myſſene rauyſſhinge thir maydens deth fatall caas pitous murdre artabanus next ordre apperyd bochas mighty duke callyd palantus sonne knight named arathus exiled though treſon ment oute cite called tarente vpon exile ſore gan compleyne beſechinge bachas gete ſpace within boke write greuous peyne albe though whilom ſtode grace glad aſpectis fortune face ſhe reyſed fauoure hir might duke eſtate pore knight • eriouſly mater conueye howe made duke gouernoure whan sperteyns gan mortally werreye ageyne myſſenys ſayth myn auctour greate coſ • age diligent laboure cauſe mighty honde rauyſſhed force maydens londe people nowe named spartenoys ſtory cleerly deuyſe call • afore lacedomynois army prouyd manly right wyſe dyd ſolempne ſacrefiſe vnto goddes people meſſenye rauyſſhed maydens coude eſpye wronge vengeaunce spartenoyſe caught indignacion aſſent hole puiſſaunce layde ſyege rounde aboute toun one wyll one affeccion made vowe ſyege whan begonne neuer departe tyll toun wonne afore toun fully ten yere laye fro ſyege made oth nat departyed nouther night daye ſtyll abode nat ſondre goth therof wyues beynge home wroth theyr huſbondes meſſangere ſent vnder theſe wordes declarynge entent sayd nat accordynge reſon lyke wydous lyue diſconſolate withoute confort conſolacion ferre huſbondys ſtonde deſolate miſcheuys conſidred fall eche eſtate longe abſence eche man ſhuld drede diuers ſekeneſſe fall womanhede tyde abide nat maner man ſtynt hir cours creature herde reherce thinge withſtonde cometh nature harme done kinde frowarde recure founde full lytell ſekirneſſe nature afforceth brotylneſſe lytell ſonde ought inough ſuffiſe declare damage may fall longe abſence folkes wiſe sumtyme departyd ageyne men may nat call ſeldom ſeen loue doth appalle thinge maketh wyues erre diſſeueraunce folke werre affect pleynly ſubſtaunce sent huſbondys ſyege laye compleynynge pleſaunce space ten yere loues playe deſolate ſorowe greate affray lyfe ladde affermynge ſentence cauſe conſtreynt longe abſence whan letter ſyege radde tofore cite mortall ſtriues aſtonyed gan wax ſadde wery almooſt lyues conſidre compleynte wyues tyll capteyne remedye oute ſought whoos counſeyle euyn thus wrought firſt olde knightes ſyege ſworne accompliſſh caſt theym true counſeyle hight beforne holde promys therfore thinge rue yonge knightes come newe myght lyſt freely wyll choſe whether wolde goo byde ſtyll herupon mooſt auayle haſt capteyne made remembraunce high prudence yaue theym counſayle knightes olde liche aſſuraunce shulde ſiege haue gouernaunce yonge knightes mooſt freſſh welbeſeyne shulde ſyege home ſent ageyne made amonge ful ſtraunge ordinaūce home comynge withoute difference entirchaunge wyues pleſaunce take hir firſt cam hir preſence accorde amonge theym ſentence mooſt redy way opynyon engendrure procreacion amonge theym quarell nouther ſtryfe matere variaunce euery man myſuſed others wyfe deſires theym pleſaunce thus child ordenaunce engendryd ca thus befall parthenoys men dyd theym call oure tunge ſpeke wordes pleyne greek liſt conſidre ſe nomore pleynly ſeyne thilke child engendred auoutrye wherfore cuntre parthenois cuſtum named borne wombes diffamed fals occaſion auoutrye cauſed greate myſcheef damage noman coude partye ſucceſſion whan cam age tytle right cleyme heritage lyne falſly doth procede harde knowe right ſhall ſuccede diſturbaunce fals ſucceſſion title cleymed afforced greate might auoutrie hath dominacion ſupported wyll nat right cleyme trouth hath loſt clere light though partyes myghty ſtronge god wilnat ſuffre ſhal endure longe parthenoyſe peiſynge theſe thinges howe fals aſſuraunce ſynage gyntill blode troubled firſt kinges man knewe high lowe parage owne fader liklyneſſe viſage fader none greate erroure coude yeue title ſucceſſoure whereupon folowed greate myſchhaunce hatefull cuntre eche man troubled countenaunce ſhulde cleyme lyberte entre londe ſtonde fre doubte eche man partie importable auoutrye greate myſcheef ſo taketh hede longe proceſſe made theym knowe ſe howe able lyklyhede outrage fall pouerte aſſent caſt theym fle vnder capiteyne ſtronge mighty honde cuntre wynne ſum londe rede chaſe duke palantus whome ſpake gouerne paſſage takinge leue ſtory telleth thus departinge begynnynge viage ſo confus cheer viſage none greate route choſe fader ſtode doute helde theym ſubſtaunce profitable euery comonte chaſe lyue exyll penanuce neuer reſorte ageyne cite ſtatutes eternyte shulde nat broke ye haue herde toforne conuencyon ſworne comon profite ſuch tendirneſſe forſoke kingdome kinrede lyue exyle ſtory bereth wytneſſe dyed lay bedrede bad bonys ſhulde caſt dede amyd theſe fer oute ſtronde ſtatutes myght ſtrength ſtonde eſchewed eueryche occaſion thinge hatefull nat fayre forſeyde royall myghty toun shulde breke othe bycauſe repayre touchinge put theym diſpaire caſt neuer reſorte dawes liſt wolde breke ſentence lawes bochas maketh exclamacion extorcion officer rome iohn bochas maketh digreſſion rebukinge caſt ſo taſſayle thilke officer rome toun extorcion oppreſſed poraile ageyne iuges alſo itayle namely theym lucre mede set trouth aſide toke none hede maketh ageyne theym exclamacion vertue contrarious vnder coloure occaſion office liſt lecherous lyke condicion vnto apius fynally ſene fals domys lif vnclene quod bochas trouth thou iuſtiſe youre nobleſſe whilom dyd excelle effect nowe excerciſe youre wonynge ala dwell practike full fewe men tell ferre put backe nowe diſciplyne youre kyn exiled youre noble lyne aduocatys nowe done occupye youre olde ſees place full royall falſhede wittes applye couetiſe nowe regneth ouer cauſes ciuile cauſes crymynall domys take fals trewe wyll ſtatutes chaunged newe eke called acceſſours syttinge iuges yeue theym counſayle may full well called rauenours nat laboure owne auayle noumbre robber folowe tayle pylle people ye haue harde toforne bare ſhepe newe ſhorne nomore mater ſeyne saue trouthſtant deſolate rightwiſneſſe dare wight compleyne wronge oppreſſed wepinge deſolate wherfore ye prince ſit high eſtate thinge amende ye better hede liſt take god ſhall full harde rekenynge make corage folke pouerte greate metys theym ſilf fede alſo ſtronge hole faire ſee alſo luſty preuyd nede vpright lymmes iourneis ſpede longe lyued cauſe expreſſe oonly none exceſſe pore men beſt medecine due laboure moderate abſtynence good aire feeldes whan phebus liſt ſhyne voidinge derke myſtes cauſe peſtilence heuy ſtomake fele violence nat enrych lechys potecaries theym ſilf ſaue vncouth let waries folkis rich werkyn contrarye theym cauſeth maladyes ſtronge dyete euery daye varye dyuers metys ſyttynge longe appetite wronge take oute tyme may nat endure cuſtum oppreſſeth nature thus myn auctour ſhortly deuiſe seeth howe glad pouert ſtandeth mooſt ſekirneſſe euyll ſeeth howe couetiſe rote grounde fals extort richeſſe ryot annexed engendringe longe ſikeneſſe theron concludynge howe moderate dyete set body ſoule moderate quiete howe enagora kinge cipre artaxe • ſes outrayed put kingdom folowynge ordre proces bochas remembreth next writynge appered reherſinge thus caas enagora cypre kinge iyen derked many folde wepinge bycauſe loſt rich londe toforne conquered honde londe cypre made mencion •• uers metallys paſſingly habounde hath richeſſe greate plente foyſon ſite like founde ſ • andith ferre ſouth many hillys rounde hath alſo many cōmeditees within boundes touns cytees touchinge cipre nomore ſeye londe enagora kinge tyll gan proudly werreye lacedomonois ꝑty bycauſe ſodeyne ciracuſe exiled twyes vengeably herte might affricans diſconfited twyes euer batayle cuſtum put flight vſaunce robbe day night lyke tyraunt ageyne conſcience ſpoyle ſubgettys rauynous violence kindred fortune wherof nat fayne hir ſtroke ageyne ſodeyne violent ſonnes two affrik firſt ſlayne lymmes wex feble impotent conſumpcion entrayles brent ague contynuall feruence ſuppryſed ſtroke peſtilence treſoure hath take proude port wordly glorye kyn freendes wif hath forſake cōqueſt dyrk put memorye name clipſed al olde victorie gan pouert diſtreſſe made ende wretchydneſſe haſty riſynge thrift ſodeyne ſurmountynge violent rauyne extort power may atteyne riche chayre lordſhip ſhyne sodeyne aſcendynge doth ſodenly declyne vntruthe euer encres men wayte cuſtum ſodeyn diſencres agathodes men may exaumple take ende euery fals tyraunt wronge clymbinge vp doth foule ende make ceſon though tirauntys puiſſaunt fortune theym yeueth lenger graunt whan ſyt hir whele mooſt royall vnware chaunge haue ſodeyne fall agathodes firſt ſimple man brought forth miſcheef pouerte sonne potter ſtory tell vicious lyuynge cam greate dignite folke hatyd cruelte clambe fro pouert vp greate richeſſe made pore ageyne dyed wretchidneſſe lenuoye ſtory ſheweth figure ſtory auctorite howe man beeſt euery creature tarageth ſtok natiuite erbe rote eche frute tre vertue alſo outrage foloweth ſome tetch taſt lynage agathodes recorde ſcripture borne lowe bed brought forth pouerte yit fortune made recure vp hye eſtate full lowe degre reſon blent cenſualite forgate ſilf ſpeke pleyne langage fals tatche cam fro lynage difference coloures picture table wall men day may ſe twene golde golde atwene bys aſure nat golde ſhyneth bright parde noble fals hath full greate beutye late men ware counterfet coignage tetchis eſchuynge chorliſſh lowe lynage sūme man forthred ſodeyne auenture set chayre royall dignite wenynge empyre euer ſhulde endure neuer troubled none aduerſite royall eglys kyte may nat fle iay may chater golden cage yit euer ſum tetch muſt folowe lynage gentyll blode royall nature euer enclyned mercy pyte cuſtum theſe vileyns cure vſurped extort fals pouſte vengeable mortall cruelte haſty fumys furious corage folowynge tetchis vileyne lynage mighty prince youre bleſſe aſſure paſſions reſt tranquillite se howe mene meſure tyraunt catchith ſouereynte late agathodes wordly myrroure eſchue tracy frowarde paſſage royall blode requereth youre lynage howe caſſander ſlough wif aliſaundre hercules hir ſonne antipater ſlough moder murder greate myſcheef fortunys might wofull fallys fro hir whele dede princys princeſſys ſo loke aright lamentable doolful rede bochas doth procede reherſayle remembringe thus ſelue apperyd men wymen twelue deth kinge agathodes cam tofore worthy queny • tweyne firſt theym called berſanes hir myſcheef gan compleyne wyf aliſaundre ſtory liſt nat feyne mighty kinge gretteſt vnder ſonne conqueſt al worlde hath wonne wif aliſaundre berſanes lyue made mencion hir ſonne named hercules caſſander brought diſtruction hir deth thoccaſion caſſandre dred berſanes quene wolde hir ſonne auengyd treſons tofore wrought aliſaundre lynage ſpecially ſhe brought macedoyne hir auauntage hir ſonne yonge age caſſander thought dred haue tolde wolde auenge treſons wrought olde caſt afore malice cauſeles caſſander mooſt falſly werkynge knight yonge hercules sonne aliſaundre recorde writinge macedoyne take crowned kinge howe wolde equite right hir faders deth auenge lyke knight thinge eſchue caſſander gan prouide fals fraude nat recheles daye liſt nat longe abide slough firſt quene ſeyde berſanes hir ſonne called hercules thus caſſander murdre crop rote murdred none bote cruelte might nat ſuffiſe vnto alyſaundre recorde ſcripture lyke tyraunt vengeable wyſe dyd theym burye frowarde auenture man ſhulde knowe ſepulture thus ala pyte rede murdryd foure one kinrede aliſaundre miniſtred poyſon slough quene called olimpiades hatrede full fals treſon haue tolde ſlough quene berſanes wife aliſaundre moder hercules youth bochas reherſinge macedoyne like haue kinge coude nat lyue pe euer redy ſome treſon slough eke quene called roxanes vpon day hir yonge ſonne ſhe wif aliſaundre alſo caſſandre dredinge opinion lyſt wolde venge vpon fals treſon thus euer lyued murdre ſorowe ſtrif way fraude cam encres finde howe wyf ſhe called theſalonices ſtory remembreth doutles ſonne borne atwene theym tweyne ſle moder dyd peyne shortly pa myn auctoure writeth none antipater hir ſonnes name cauſe ſhe louyd brother better greate diffame compaſſed hir deth ſtory ſeyth ſame natwithſtandinge tappeſe cruelte aſkyd mercy knelinge hir kne hir breſtys open white ſoft ſilke bedewed • yrys hir viſake requeryd mekely reuerence milke foſtred yonge age haue mercy tappeſe rage accepte goodly hir prayere ſaue lyf moder dere nought herde hir neueradell hir ſurmountinge meſure lyke fader vengeable cruell trowe • nature recorde kinde eke ſcripture seelde neuer braunch good springeth cuſtome oute crue • blode hir deth cauſe none antipater ſlou • 〈◊〉 moder dere ſhe loued al • 〈◊〉 brother better cronicle doth v lere aliſaundre ye liſt concluſion brynge demetrius deſtruction one firſte worthy tholome kynge egypt armes full famous othir tweyne ſtory ye may ſe called selenchus next liſymachus cipre cam kynge pirthus lorde prouince eke founde made theym ſtronge demetrius cōfounde shortly tell apparayles macedoyne dyd firſt depryue cam vpon foure ſtronge batayles neuer ſo ouerſet lyue take lyſymachus ſtory doth deſcryue cheyned gan werre agayne make fayne lordſhips forſake howe ſandrodoctus borne lowe degre cheriſſhed robbours theues oter prefectis alſo finde helde people full greate ſeruage macedoyne outher ynde tyll ſandrodoctus man lowe lyuage caſt wolde redreſſe outrage entent pore people reſtore fraunchiſes playned ſore sandrodoctus auctoure werkinge behight peple throughoute cuntrees whan ſleyght crowned iohn bochas greate aduerſite terys bedewed hir viſage gan compleyne conſtreynt hir rage mighty quene ſayde arcynoe ſonnys tweyne full famous renoun tone lyſymachus excellinge beute tothyr philip made mencion hir ioye dilectacion wordly blyſſe nomore feyne hooly ſet vpon theſe child tweyne thoccaſion greate fayreneſſe men delited greatly theym ſe namely wymen ſtory doth expreſſe moder quene arcenoe stode greate hope ſhuld mighty kingis iuſt ſucceſſion macedoyne mighty region title faders right hir herte gaue full greate gladneſſe ſhe dempt none wight ſuccede ſhulde haue none intereſſe fortune blinde fals goddeſſe diſpoſyd ſo child tweyne none theym purpos ſhulde atteyne whan fader lyſymachus ſlayne ſayde quene called arcynoe ſaue hir lif coude none gayne hir ſonnys feerfully fle •• caſſander mighty ſtronge cyte • ly drede one antigonus theym purſued ſtory telleth thus brother quene arcynoe called ceramyus reſcued hir partye ageyne antigonus ye may ſtory ſe yi • herte greate enuye albe nere one allye hir two ſonnys ſhulde kinges macedoyne regne cuntre ſette couetiſe crowned macedoyne kinge fals treſon ſtory doth diuiſe theym deſceyue werkinge firſt quene full humbly knelinge made promys vnder great ſurete macedoyne ſhe ſhulde crowned hir child ſo faire viſage shulde kept vnder gouernaunce vnto tyme come age put hir aſſuraunce ceramius ſwore god yeue ſory chaunce purpoſed fals werkinge crowne hir quene make hir ſonnes kinges toke goddys vnto witneſſe ſwore ageyne pleyne viſage vnto quene fraude doubleneſſe purpos haue hir mariage crowne hir quene hir greate auauntage thus ſworne though hir brother yit herte god wote thought another vnder coloure aſſuraunce lete entre caſſandre cyte cam ageyne pleſaunce hir lordes hye lowe degre made ſtretys hangyd clothis golde ſolempne wyſe goddys dyd ſacrifiſe thus receyued ſolemply day halowed holde feſtyuall quene ioye ordeyned richely hir two ſonnys ſo faire crowned crownes full royall goo afore hir maiſter ſtrete gloriouſly vncle mete felonous herte vnder frendly face ceranius rote treſon gan coſyns benigly enbrace purpoſinge fals colluſion procede deſtruction finally firſt dyd peyne quene exyle ſle hir child twyne treſon brout preef whan quene apperceyued falſneſſe ſawe hir ſonnys brought ſuch miſcheef coniured hir mortall diſtreſſe haue pyte naturall gentylneſſe spare coſyns afore ſtode royall mercy ſo nere borne blode crye paſſynge lamentable fyll afore ſwownynge vnto grounde lyke ſhe verely coupable seynge hir ſonnys bledynge many wounde nought mercy founde blode ſtory nat feyned hir garnement doolfully deſteyned hir face faire ſoyled ordure hir golden torne rent like thrall woofull creature mortall wepynge hir ſight blent fynde howe ſhe ſent burye hir child ſpace yle called samontrace ſtory maketh mencion princeſſe ſo hye degre fonde ſo greate cauſe lamentacion beynge doughter greate tholome hir child ſlayne vengeable cruelte beholde deth mooſt dolorous hir huſbonde called lyſymachus banyſſhed exile made hir ende ſorowfull conpleynt hir lif thus drawe alonge tyll fate hir ſprite dyd wende drede hir peynes full ſtronge ſhulde reherce wronge ſhe ſuffred wolde greue cheuyſaunce moder exiled callyd arcynoe noble princis ware hye prudence amonge youre ſilf diſtaunce hyde rancoure hatfull violence vnder curteyne double daliaunce lyke herte ſhewe countenaunce vayde compleyneth pyte quaking hande whā pen toke gan write woful deſtenye ye haue herde quene arcynoe howe ceramyus ſtory maketh mynde hir fals traytoure vnkinde whoos treſon made greate proceſſe howe ſlayne batayle punyſſhed vengeaunce greate falſneſſe lyke ſtory maketh reherſayle remembre caſt nat fayle folowynge myn auctoure procede writynge howe ceramyus ſlayne whan kynge fals werkynge macedoyne gouernayle thre hundryd thouſande accounted wrytinge went oute fraunce conquere itayle hoſt departyd many ſtronge batayle gate conqueſt hye renoun full many prouince many region rode many greate cuntre people gaule ſtele armyd clene founded caſtels many ſtronge cyte towarde rome bilded mylan sene vpon talpies armoure ſhone full ſhene ſūme theym vp rome went force cyte brent sūme quyk theyr deth full ſodeyne ſacrefyſe goddys gan diſdeyn ramayns wex contraryous fals rightys ſuperſticious recorde olde croniculeers yere fyue hundre fro fundacion one twenty tho beynge conſulers preſerue aduerſite ageyn two peples gaule lumberdye werred malyce enuye werre romayns ſtode boute ſenatours citeſeyns bycauſe ageynſt cam ſo great route lumbardys halfe mounteyns ioyned togedre many fell foreyns ſtode departed made remembraunce fro rome obeyſaunce people rude beſtyall vnſtable togedre aſſemblyd wode furious multitude innumerable vengeable herte corage deſpytous voyde reſon ſodeynly furious ſeyth bochas ferther gone ſoudiours bare giſarmys euerychon gyſarmes giſarmes called towarde rome haſtinge day day greate laboure fotemen ſore app • llyd ay truſte multitude lay whoos comynge rome ſtode afray ſpecially conſuleers thre ſent fight cite foure ſcore thouſand write croniclere mighty ſtonde diffence felawſhip eche conſulere giſarmes noumbre ſentence thre hundred thouſande ſturdy violence goynge fote finde eight thouſand ouer feeld ſpred rekne nat rode horſbak ſix thretty thouſand noumbre sixe hundryd ouer purpoſed wrak fynally romayns encoumbre ſhadowe gaue ſo great vmbre ſoyle tofore grene enneth ſonne ſhene capteyne abitomarus manly man full worthy knight went viridomarus another capteyne ſtele armyd bright twene romayns longe laſt fight party rome cite ſlayne conſull one thre whoos deth fortune anone right party rome toun eyght hundred thouſande toke flight thus began fame renoun abithomarus made mencion victorye herte made fayne partye thre thouſand ſlayne romayns reſorted agayn ſtronge batale feeld ſo manly ſeyne ſo proudly enmyes dyd aſſayle myn auctour maketh reherſayle gyſarmys longe night fourty thauſand ſlayne fight thrydde tyme help fraunce ioyned lumbardes folke gaule alſo faught ageyne oute ordenaunce beſide ryuere callyd poo batayles togydre adoo fynde conſulers tweyne romayn ſheltrouns knightly dyd ordeyne maulius torquat called one flamynus flakkus ifere romayns forth gydre gon towarde ryuere full manly chere bataile ſtory doth v lere nyne fourty thouſand ſlayne day enmyes none ne went away abythomarus takyn pryſonere tokne tryumphe brought rome toun capitoyle full pale chere led bounde chenys gayned raunſon thus hath fortune appallyd hye renoun tokne diſconfiture offred goddys cote armure thus lacheſis lyues threde gan drawe tyll antropos brak full greate peyne viridomarus felawe slayn felde romayns certeyne theſe worthy prince tweyne ende mortall fall feeſt accompliſſhid callyd funerall tyme theſe mortall werres atwene theſe duke rome toun many toknes ſhewed ſterres meruaylous lightnynges fro heuen doun many vncouth conſtellacion sondry cometes dyd walkinge appere ſeth ſtoryes may trouth lere water pytene renneth itayle cuntre famous flode ſame houre tyme batayle ſeith ſtory turned blode fyres heyre mooſt furious wode mighty toures flamys brent thre monys apperinge orient peple fere fled lowe caues drede wex pale dedly chere thre dayes thre erth quauys duringe weres ſame yere great appollo fyll doun pyllere marbyll white large great ſtrength ſixty cubites accoumted lengethe tyme ſtory ſayth nat nay rome conſull great puiſſaunce callyd claudius ſlough vpon day thretty thouſand brought miſchaunce ſoudiours cam fraunce ſlayne many captayn lorne virydomarus ſpak toforne greate ſhame confuſion remembryd ſcripture romayns made great oblacion vp iupiter cote armure tokne diſconfiture within temple golde betyn clere deſpyte henge vp banere howe siphax munedye kinge take dyed priſon bochas breuely remembraunce writeth werres debate batayles tyme itayle fraunce ſpayne chaūpayne marciall apparayles amonge reherſayles telleth affrik great diſſencion atwene hanyball worthy scipion toucheth name abydeth nat longe vpon ſtoryes byde nat awhile nat reherſinge mighty werrys ſtronge ſtryues doth nat compyle doun deſſendynge dyrecteth furth ſtyle reherce tell writynge fall siphax munedye kinge ſaide siphax batayles tweyne one kinge gabba might eke dyd payne mete maſmiſſa anon right kinges put flight meſſulie fynde writinge howe maſmiſſa gouernour kynge ſayd ſiphax thrugh chiualrye made maſmyſſa fle region conſtreynyd lyue robbrye walke foreſtys beſtys vp doun diffaute made mencion ſaue lyf fonde better refute fed ſilf rotys frute oute realme maſmyſſa enchaſyd conſtreyned fle fro cuntre fro mynde folke name raced man wyſte ſhulde liege men folke cyte affryk knewe better rede perſone dempt dede thus kynge siphax encrece gan glorye force two kinges hath outrayed vpon wonne victorye put flight peple affrayed rome cartage diſmayed eche theym dyd laboure werrys make gouernoure vnto siphax rome toun wretyn memoriall numedye ſent ſcipion mater eſpeciall cartage ſent haſtruball caſtell siphax lay tweyne arryued one day pleyne writinge haue conceyued ſtory remembreth ſentence cūmynge receyued kinge shyhax greate reuerence notable manly diligence wretyn gode recorde made theſe capteyns hertely acorde gedre lay ſame night syphax ſo greate ſuerte promyſe made true knight nouther ſhulde deceyuyd founde greate duplycyte folowynge ſo take hede lyke ſtorye ſhall deuyſe dede fraude falſnes moſte mortall compaſſed beforn thus befall ſleight haſtruball affricans nye double vnder ſuger hide well gall haſtruball fals decepcion vnder fayre chere deſceyued scipion brought ſiphax fals ſubtylte ſleyght peyntyd fayre langage ſhulde allyed full aſſente haue mariage sophaniſba maydyn cartage doughter yonge faire withall ſeyth bochas haſtruball thinge craft brought aboute accompliſſhed verely dede mene pleynly doute firſt began rancoure hatrede symulacion feynyd falſhede atwene ſiphax haſtruball ala scipion diceyued ca done mariage syphax full enmye scipion haſtruball rode cartage gan werraye agayn rome toun made mencion kynge maſmyſſa wilderneſſe towarde scipion haſte gan dreſſe people gan make ſtronge helpe ſcipion bellius went ageyne ſyphax abode nat longe herte ageyne ſo enuyous day ſtory telleth thus affricans folkys cartage siphax romayns met viſage maſmyſſa peple ſo wode vpon siphax auengyd batayles cam ſtode maugre cruelte manhode ſpace none fle brought home thrugh hye renoun hondys worthy scipion siphax take thus ware vnder baner maugre might rome led afore chare ſcipion noble worthy knight wan triumphe graunted right siphoniſba afore sophax wif wed maſmyſſe ende ſtrif loo howe fortune chaunge hir tydes one day ſhe fauorable make capteyns theſe greate guydes wend haue founde hir whele ſtable ſhe ay frowarde chaungeable frendly day tomorowe diſcorde true siphax bere recorde shiphax ſent toun cheynes bounde without taryinge tyburny lay fetred priſon dyed miſcheef made ther endynge bycauſe kinge romayns made marciall pyte buried within cite howe nabyn hauyng title tyrannye toke kinge macedoyne ſlayne next cam nabyn full pytouſly wepynge tofore iohn bochas tyrannye macedoyne toke kinge hauynge title ſaue title robbrye force ſilf magnefye ſtronge honde toke full poſſeſſion crownyd thilke region macedoyne olde writinges whilom full great reuerence bycauſe floured two thinges knighthode ſouereyne ſapience mar manhode pallas prudence theſe tweyne gouernaunce welfare ſuffiſaunce nobleſſe theſe thinges tweyne ſey floure hye clergye hye renoun moſte famous ſouereyne marciall proweſſe chiualrye gouerned londe newe pollicie ſtode kingdom auctours reherce kōne amonge grekys lyke heuenly ſonne laſte eclipſed light knighthode philoſophye whan couetiſe gan entre ageyne right vſurpe caas therby knighthode fully tranſlated policye cronycles ye may ſe grece rome cyte amonge clere remembraunce ſuch tyrauntys ordre reherſinge nabyn one gouernaunce macedoyne ther crounyd kynge without tytle falſly regnynge frowarde contagious cruelte behatyd rome cyte romayns ſent mighty conſulere titus flamynius werres guide macedoyne gan approch nere towarde argo nabyn dyd abyde entente abate pryde nabyn ſtode hyeſt eſtate grece liege debate duke callyd pilopomones people dwelled grece londe ſtryue nabyn put ſilf pres diſconfited fightinge honde honde greate miſcheef ye ſhall vnderſtond alexamenes knight cuntre slough nabyn cronicle ye may ſe bochas reherceth mortall werrys betwene romayns affricans nabyn bochas doth procede tell warrys mortal ſtryues twene romayns affricans dede wherby full many loſte lyues cauſyd wedowes maydyns eke wyues wepe weyle ſuch diſioynt ſtode outher party ſe loſſe blode party rome toun made capteyns diuers officeers affrik peple ſent doun ſpecially ther two conſuleers notable army famous tho yeres marcus maulius borne romayn lyne called lucius cenſoryne theym ſent tribune full notable tofore made mencion werres mooſt worthy mooſt able mene rome proude scipion cite cheueſt champion entent affricans tanoye ſpecially cartage deſtroye nye cartage ther cyte ſtronge mightely bilded ſtode vpon ſe wally thicke rounde ſquare longe cheef diffence callyd cuntre ſaue kepe aduerſite fourty cubites creeſtys marciall lyke fynde hight wall fronte reyſed werre ſtonys ſquare hye dungeon called birſa fro wonder ferre men might beholde cuntrees enuiron mighty ſtronge ſure force knight mooſt marciall great quantite brake doun wall lucius called senſoryne deꝑtyd marchus maulius counſayle ſcipion doctrine aſſente army vertuous toke wey myn auctour obeyſaunce theym rome withoute excepcion greate lordys mooſt puiſſaunce abode ther longe vnder gouernaunce perſeus diſconſolat chere durynge lif abode pryſonere howe people af achaia cheef cyte corinthe romaynes deſtroyed thus lordſhip weryd ſpent macedoyne made mencion two cuntrees therto adiacent one achaia lytyll region ſpatanoys goynge enuyron mighty people greate ſubſtaunce one confederat one alliaunce conioyned made al one manere feithfull conuencion whan romayns knewe theym fone hauynge frenſhip ſuſpeccion caſte make diſiunction bytwene theſe londes brede eke length thinge diſſeueryd menuſed ſtrength ordeyned cytes townes yonder wheron romaynes gan make decre lordſhippes ſhulde ſet aſſonder made people euery greate cyte whan knewe ſubtilte ryſe onys mooſt cruell cheris achaia negligence frowarde wylfull recheleſneſſe pryde liſt make diffence thought ſilf without auyſeneſſe power able ſtrenger ſothneſſe romayns verely dede thus ſtroyed afore toke hede ſtode hope cheef cite deſtroyed romaynes brought ruine amonge cytees bochas ye may ſee aboue dyd honoure ſhyne ſciences floured doctryne craftes artifycers mooſt wyſe rekne worlde cheef marchaundyſe thus vnwarly mooſt nobleſſe sittynge fortune ſtage deſtroyed treſoure richeſſe brought nought ſlaughter pyllage walles broke cruell rage brennynge bochas ſeith leuene raught greate part vpwarde heuene pleyne erth romaynes great ambaſſatrye ſeyde marchus trete pe • ambaſſet doutles whan atteyned marchus preſence refuſed none audience antiochus greatly aſhamyd caſt ageyne rome hate enmyte reyſe power hath newe aſſygned tutoure ſe vpon gouernaunce full power lorde emperoure empyre vndre obeyſaunce princys lordes gaue attendaunce preſent abſent ech thynge done commaundement mene thus honde conſtantynople cyte great ſubſtaunce extorcyons dyd londe ſubgettes miſgouernaunce amonge lordes fyll remembraunce aſſent herte gan deſire call andronycus ageyn empyre aſſent reſtored crownyd emperoure conſtantynople entrynge cyte byſyed fraudolent laboure blode born imperiall ſe ſlayne vengeable cruelte iugement andronycus exepte prince called iſacyus thus effect trouth well ſeyn vengeable laſt oldeage right yerys grene felly gouerned full fals outrage laſte malicious corage toke counceile grece thus named ſuch diſclaundryd diffamed homecydes houſholde tyrauntes wrought ageyn rightwyſneſſe cheriſſhed violence vice youth dyd enclyne royall lyne ſlayn echon except iſacyus tolde erſt andronycus fynde haſt ſent purpos come preſence murdre entente dyuers toknes many euydence fully knewe fyne ſentence lyke prince lyſt come nonere smet hede meſſangere manly prouydence myd cyte ſhewyd lyke knight prayde lordes yeue audyence princys iuges right might declare ſight great iniuryes damage outragyous wrought emperoure callyd andronycus citezyns knowe guyſe emperour called andronycus nat emperoure ſo ye lyſt aduertiſe tyraunt cruell furrous fals mordrere vengeable diſpytous hath newe frowarde fals corage slayn empyre holy lynage lyue left none blode saue alone royall lyne andronycus lyke tyraunt wode hath ſlayn echon brefly termyne ſwerde vengeaunce might nat declyne nowe purpoſeth mortall tyrannye sle alſo alye requirynge conſiſtorye cytezyns preſent remembre call memorye howe famous imperiall cite hath ay ben redy equite beſy alſo nobleſſe wronge tyrauntes manly oppreſſe philoſophers poetys eke deuyſe ſawes prudent notable blode tyrauntes noble ſacrifyſe god aboue whan vengeable ſith ye rightfull iuſt ſtable youre werkys voyde varyaunce weye matere iuſtly balaunce peple echon one aſſent outrage thys andronycus put doun rightfull iugement whoos place ſet vp iſacius ſayde tyraunte frowarde vicious gan maligne theym ſilf dreſſe diffence make fortereſſe holpe nat make reſiſtence woman religion made wyues breke profeſſion violence peyſe well thinge right requireth haue euyll endynge mooſt murdre contagious innocent blode make effuſion vengeable alſo ageyn vertuous ageyns
